VISTAVIEW - useNavStack Hook\n// Navigation breadcrumb tracking for voice \"go back\" commands\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n\nimport { useState, useCallback } from 'react';\n\ninterface NavItem {\n  id: string;\n  label: string;\n  data?: any;\n}\n\nexport const useNavStack = (initial: NavItem) => {\n  const [stack, setStack] = useState<NavItem[]>([initial]);\n\n  const push = useCallback((item: NavItem) => {\n    setStack(prev => [...prev, item]);\n  }, []);\n\n  const pop = useCallback(() => {\n    setStack(prev => prev.length > 1 ? prev.slice(0, -1) : prev);\n    return stack[stack.length - 2] || null;\n  }, [stack]);\n\n  const reset = useCallback(() => {\n    setStack([initial]);\n  }, [initial]);\n\n  const current = stack[stack.length - 1];\n  const canGoBack = stack.length > 1;\n  const breadcrumbs = stack.map(s => s.label);\n\n  return { stack, current, canGoBack, breadcrumbs, push, pop, reset };\n};\n\nexport default useNavStack;\nEOF\n\necho \"  \u2705 useNavStack.ts created\"\n\n# React, { useState, useCallback, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';\nimport AgentBar from '../common/AgentBar';\nimport { useVoice } from '../common/useVoice';\nimport { useNavStack } from '../common/useNavStack';\nimport VendorPhone from './VendorPhone';\nimport VendorOTP from './VendorOTP';\nimport VendorProfile from './VendorProfile';\nimport VendorDashboard from './VendorDashboard';\nimport VendorUpload from './VendorUpload';\nimport VendorPipeline from './VendorPipeline';\n\ninterface VendorFlowProps {\n  isOpen: boolean;\n  onClose: () => void;\n  onComplete: () => void;\n  onBack: () => void;\n}\n\ntype Step = 'phone' | 'otp' | 'profile' | 'dashboard' | 'upload' | 'pipeline' | 'complete';\n\nconst STEPS: { id: Step; label: string }[] = [\n  { 'pipeline', label: 'Processing' },\n  { id: 'complete', label: 'Complete' }\n];\n\nconst THEME = { teal: '#004236', gold: '#B8860B', goldLight: '#F5EC9B' };\n\nconst VendorFlow: React.FC<VendorFlowProps> = ({ isOpen, onClose, onComplete, onBack }) => {\n  const [step, setStep] = useState<Step>('phone');\n  const [vendorData, setVendorData] = useState({\n    phone: '',\n Handle voice commands\n  const handleCommand = useCallback((cmd: string) => {\n    console.log('[VendorFlow] Command:', cmd, 'Step:', step);\n    const c = cmd.toLowerCase();\n\n    // Global commands\n    if (c.includes('stop') || c.includes('quiet')) { voice.stop(); return; }\n    if (c.includes('close') || c.includes('exit')) { voice.stop(); onClose(); return; }\n    if (c.includes('back') || c.includes('go back')) { goBack(); return; }\n    if (c.includes('next') || c.includes('continue')) { goNext(); return; }\n\n    // Step-specific\n    if (step === 'phone' && (c.includes('yes') || c.includes('correct'))) {\n      if (vendorData.phone.length >= 10) {\n        goToStep('otp');\n        voice.speak(\"Sending code. Enter 1 2 3 4 5 6 for demo.\");\n      }\n    }\n    if (step === 'profile' && (c.includes('save') || c.includes('beautify'))) {\n      if (c.includes('beautify')) voice.speak(\"Enhancing your profile...\");\n      else saveProfile();\n    }\n    if (step === 'dashboard' && (c.includes('upload') || c.includes('catalog'))) {\n      goToStep('upload');\n      voice.speak(\"Upload your catalog. I accept PDF, Excel, or CSV.\");\n    }\n    if (step === 'complete') {\n      if (c.includes('view') || c.includes('product')) onComplete();\n      if (c.includes('done') || c.includes('finish')) onClose();\n    }\n  }, [step, vendorData.phone, onClose, onComplete]);\n\n  // Handle voice digits - pass to child\n  const handleDigits = useCallback((digits: string) => {\n    console.log('[VendorFlow] Digits:', digits);\n    voiceDigitHandlerRef.current?.(digits);\n  }, []);\n\n  const voice = useVoice({ onCommand: handleCommand, onDigits: handleDigits, autoStart: isOpen });\n\n  // Navigation helpers\n  const goBack = () => {\n    const order: Step[] = ['phone', 'otp', 'profile', 'dashboard', 'upload', 'pipeline'];\n    const idx = order.indexOf(step);\n    if (idx <= 0) { onBack(); return; }\n    const prev = order[idx - 1];\n    setStep(prev);\n    navStack.pop();\n    voice.speak(`Going back to ${STEPS.find(s => s.id === prev)?.label}.`);\n  };\n\n  const goNext = () => {\n    const order: Step[] = ['phone', 'otp', 'profile', 'dashboard', 'upload', 'pipeline', 'complete'];\n    const idx = order.indexOf(step);\n    if (idx < order.length - 1) {\n      const next = order[idx + 1];\n      goToStep(next);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const goToStep = (newStep: Step) => {\n    navStack.push({ id: `vendor:${newStep}`, label: STEPS.find(s => s.id === newStep)?.label || newStep });\n    setStep(newStep);\n  };\n\n  // Save profile to backend\n  const saveProfile = async () => {\n    voice.speak(\"Saving your profile...\");\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch('http://localhost:1117/api/vendors', {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        body: JSON.stringify({\n          phone: vendorData.phone,\n          profile: vendorData.beautifiedProfile || vendorData.profile,\n          companyName: vendorData.companyName,\n          createdAt: new Date().toISOString()\n        })\n      });\n      const data = await res.json();\n      setVendorData(d => ({ ...d, vendorId: data.id }));\n      goToStep('dashboard');\n      voice.speak(\"Profile saved! Welcome to your dashboard. Say upload catalog to add products.\");\n    } catch (e) {\n      console.error('Save failed:', e);\n      goToStep('dashboard');\n      voice.speak(\"Profile saved locally. Say upload catalog to continue.\");\n    }\n  };\n\n  // Format phone for display\n  const formatPhone = (d: string) => {\n    const c = d.replace(/\\D/g, '').slice(0, 10);\n    if (c.length <= 3) return c;\n    if (c.length <= 6) return `${c.slice(0, 3)}-${c.slice(3)}`;\n    return `${c.slice(0, 3)}-${c.slice(3, 6)}-${c.slice(6)}`;\n  };\n\n  // Welcome on open\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (isOpen && step === 'phone') {\n      setTimeout(() => {\n        voice.speak(\"Welcome Vendor! Tell me your phone number, say each digit clearly.\");\n      }, 500);\n    }\n  }, [isOpen]);\n\n  // Cleanup\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (!isOpen) {\n      voice.stop();\n      voice.stopListening();\n      setStep('phone');\n    }\n  }, [isOpen]);\n\n  if (!isOpen) return null;\n\n  const stepIndex = STEPS.findIndex(s => s.id === step);\n  const canGoBack = step !== 'phone';\n\n  return (\n    <div style={{ position: 'fixed', inset: 0, background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.92)', zIndex: 10000, display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', alignItems: 'center', padding: '20px' }}>\n      <div style={{ background: `linear-gradient(135deg, ${THEME.teal}, #001a15)`, borderRadius: '20px', width: '100%', maxWidth: '850px', maxHeight: '92vh', overflow: 'hidden', border: `2px solid ${THEME.gold}40`, display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column' }}>\n        \n        {/* Header */}\n        <div style={{ padding: '16px 24px', background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)', borderBottom: `1px solid ${THEME.gold}30`, display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center' }}>\n          <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '14px' }}>\n            <span style={{ fontSize: '1.6em' }}>\ud83d\udce6</span>\n            <div>\n              <h2 style={{ color: '#fff', margin: 0, fontSize: '1.1em' }}>Vendor Setup</h2>\n              <span style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: '0.8em' }}>Step {stepIndex + 1} of {STEPS.length - 1}</span>\n            </div>\n          </div>\n          <button onClick={onClose} style={{ background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)', border: 'none', color: '#fff', width: '36px', height: '36px', borderRadius: '50%', cursor: 'pointer', fontSize: '1.2em' }}>\u2715</button>\n        </div>\n\n        {/* Progress Bar */}\n        <div style={{ display: 'flex', padding: '10px 24px', gap: '4px', background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.2)' }}>\n          {STEPS.slice(0, -1).map((s, i) => (\n            <div key={s.id} style={{ flex: 1, height: '4px', borderRadius: '2px', background: stepIndex >= i ? THEME.gold : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.15)' }} />\n          ))}\n        </div>\n\n        {/* Agent Bar with Teleprompter */}\n        <AgentBar\n          isListening={voice.isListening}\n          isSpeaking={voice.isSpeaking}\n          isPaused={voice.isPaused}\n          transcript={voice.transcript}\n          displayText={voice.displayText}\n          onStop={voice.stop}\n          onPause={voice.pause}\n          onResume={voice.resume}\n          onBack={goBack}\n          onClose={onClose}\n          canGoBack={canGoBack}\n          showModes={true}\n          showNavButtons={true}\n        />\n\n        {/* Content */}\n        <div style={{ flex: 1, overflow: 'auto', padding: '24px' }}>\n          {step === 'phone' && (\n            <VendorPhone\n              value={vendorData.phone}\n              onChange={(phone) => setVendorData(d => ({ ...d, phone }))}\n              onNext={() => { goToStep('otp'); voice.speak(`Sending code to ${vendorData.phone}. Enter 1 2 3 4 5 6 for demo.`); }}\n              speak={voice.speak}\n              onVoiceDigits={(handler) => { voiceDigitHandlerRef.current = handler; }}\n            />\n          )}\n          {step === 'otp' && (\n            <VendorOTP\n              phone={formatPhone(vendorData.phone)}\n              onVerified={() => { goToStep('profile'); voice.speak(\"Verified! Tell me about your business.\"); }}\n              speak={voice.speak}\n              onVoiceDigits={(handler) => { voiceDigitHandlerRef.current = handler; }}\n            />\n          )}\n          {step === 'profile' && (\n            <VendorProfile\n              profile={vendorData.profile}\n              beautified={vendorData.beautifiedProfile}\n              companyName={vendorData.companyName}\n              onChange={(p) => setVendorData(d => ({ ...d, profile: p }))}\n              onCompanyChange={(n) => setVendorData(d => ({ ...d, companyName: n }))}\n              onBeautify={(b) => setVendorData(d => ({ ...d, beautifiedProfile: b }))}\n              onSave={saveProfile}\n              speak={voice.speak}\n            />\n          )}\n          {step === 'dashboard' && (\n            <VendorDashboard\n              vendorName={vendorData.companyName || 'Your Store'}\n              onUploadCatalog={() => { goToStep('upload'); voice.speak(\"Upload your catalog. I'll process and publish your products.\"); }}\n              speak={voice.speak}\n            />\n          )}\n          {step === 'upload' && (\n            <VendorUpload\n              onFileSelected={(file) => {\n                setVendorData(d => ({ ...d, catalogFile: file }));\n                goToStep('pipeline');\n                voice.speak(`Processing ${file.name}. You can browse the homepage while I work. I'll notify you when done.`);\n              }}\n              speak={voice.speak}\n            />\n          )}\n          {step === 'pipeline' && (\n            <VendorPipeline\n              fileName={vendorData.catalogFile?.name}\n              onComplete={(products) => {\n                setVendorData(d => ({ ...d, products }));\n                setStep('complete');\n                voice.speak(\"Congratulations! Your catalog is now live on VistaView!\");\n              }}\n              speak={voice.speak}\n              onBrowseHome={() => voice.speak(\"Feel free to browse. I'll keep processing.\")}\n            />\n          )}\n          {step === 'complete' && (\n            <div style={{ textAlign: 'center', padding: '40px 20px' }}>\n              <div style={{ width: '100px', height: '100px', borderRadius: '50%', background: 'linear-gradient(135deg, #4CAF50, #2E7D32)', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', margin: '0 auto 24px', boxShadow: '0 0 30px rgba(76,175,80,0.4)' }}>\n                <span style={{ fontSize: '3em', color: '#fff' }}>\u2713</span>\n              </div>\n              <h3 style={{ color: THEME.gold, marginBottom: '12px' }}>\ud83c\udf89 You're Live!</h3>\n              <p style={{ color: '#aaa', marginBottom: '32px' }}>{vendorData.products?.length || 0} products published</p>\n              <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '12px', justifyContent: 'center', flexWrap: 'wrap' }}>\n                <button onClick={onComplete} style={{ padding: '14px 32px', background: THEME.gold, color: '#000', border: 'none', borderRadius: '25px', cursor: 'pointer', fontWeight: 600 }}>\ud83d\udce6 View Products</button>\n                <button onClick={onClose} style={{ padding: '14px 24px', background: 'transparent', color: '#888', border: '1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.2)', borderRadius: '25px', cursor: 'pointer' }}>Done</button>\n              </div>\n            </div>\n          )}\n        </div>\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  );\n};\n\nexport default VendorFlow;\nEOF\n\necho \"  \u2705 VendorFlow.tsx MAIN ORCHESTRATOR created\"\n\n# \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n\nimport   { name: 'Home Decor', icon: '\ud83c\udfe0', style: 'IKEA' },\n    { name: 'Lighting', icon: '\ud83d\udca1', style: 'Wayfair' },\n    { name: 'Kitchen', icon: '\ud83c\udf73', style: 'Williams-Sonoma' },\n    { name: 'Bath', icon: '\ud83d\udebf', style: 'Bed Bath' },\n    { name: 'Outdoor', icon: '\ud83c\udf33', style: 'Home Depot' }\n  ],\n  priceRanges: ['Under $50', '$50-$200', '$200-$500', '$500+'],\n  sortOptions: ['Featured', 'Price: Low to High', 'Price: High to Low', 'Newest', 'Best Rated']\n};\n\nconst ProductCatalog: React.FC<Props> = ({ isOpen, onClose }) => {\n  const [view, useState<string[]>([]);\n\n  // Voice command handler\n  const handleCommand = useCallback((cmd: string) => {\n    console.log('[Catalog] Voice command:', cmd);\n    const c = cmd.toLowerCase();\n\n    // Navigation commands\n    if (c.includes('close') || c.includes('exit') || c.includes('back')) {\n      if (view === 'detail') { setView('products'); setSelectedProduct(null); voice.speak(\"Going back to products.\"); }\n      else if (view === 'products') { setView('vendors'); setSelectedVendor(null); voice.speak(\"Going back to vendors.\"); }\n      else { onClose(); }\n      return;\n    }\n\n    // Category commands\n    for (const cat of AI_PATTERNS.categories) {\n      if (c.includes(cat.name.toLowerCase())) {\n        setSelectedCategory(cat.name);\n        voice.speak(`Showing ${cat.name} products, ${cat.style} style.`);\n        return;\n      }\n    }\n\n    // Search commands\n    if (c.includes('search') || c.includes('find')) {\n      const query = c.replace(/search|find|for/gi, '').trim();\n      if (query) {\n        setSearchQuery(query);\n        voice.speak(`Searching for ${query}.`);\n      }\n      return;\n    }\n\n    // View vendor\n    if (c.includes('vendor') || c.includes('store')) {\n      const vendorName = c.replace(/show|view|open|vendor|store/gi, '').trim();\n      const v = vendors.find(v => v.companyName.toLowerCase().includes(vendorName));\n      if (v) {\n        selectVendor(v);\n      } else {\n        voice.speak(\"Which vendor would you like to see? Say the name.\");\n      }\n      return;\n    }\n\n    // Product selection by number\n    const num = parseInt(c.match(/\\d+/)?.[0] || '');\n    if (!isNaN(num) && num > 0 && num <= products.length) {\n      selectProduct(products[num - 1]);\n      return;\n    }\n\n    // AI insights\n    if (c.includes('insight') || c.includes('recommend') || c.includes('suggest')) {\n      generateAIInsights();\n      return;\n    }\n\n    // Stop speaking\n    if (c.includes('stop') || c.includes('quiet')) {\n      voice.stop();\n      return;\n    }\n  }, [view, vendors, products, onClose]);\n\n  const voice = useVoice({ onCommand: handleCommand, autoStart: isOpen });\n\n  // Fetch vendors\n  const fetchVendors = async () => {\n    setLoading(true);\n    try {\n      const res fetch('http://localhost:1117/api/ai/training/stats');\n      const aiData = await aiRes.json();\n      if (aiData.patterns) {\n        setAiInsights(aiData.patterns.slice(0, 3));\n      }\n    } catch (e) {\n      console.error('Fetch vendors failed:', e);\n      // Mock data\n      setVendors([\n        { id: 'v1', companyName: 'Premium Tiles Co', productCount: 24 },\n        { id: 'v2', companyName: 'Modern Fixtures', productCount: 18 },\n        { id: 'v3', companyName: 'Eco Home Supplies', productCount: 32 }\n      ]);\n    }\n    setLoading(false);\n  };\n\n  // Fetch products for vendor\n  const fetchProducts = async (vendorId: string) => {\n    setLoading(true);\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`http://localhost:1117/api/vendors/${vendorId}/products`);\n      const data = await res.json();\n      setProducts(data || []);\n    } catch (e) {\n      // Mock products with AI-style descriptions\n      setProducts([\n        { id: 'p1', name: 'Premium Ceramic Tile', price: 89.99, category: 'Flooring', vendor: selectedVendor?.companyName || '', vendorId, description: 'Inspired by Nebraska Furniture quality standards' },\n        { id: 'p2', name: 'Modern LED Fixture', price: 149.99, category: 'Lighting', vendor: selectedVendor?.companyName || '', vendorId, description: 'IKEA-style minimalist design' },\n        { id: 'p3', name: 'Eco Bamboo Cabinet', price: 299.99, category: 'Furniture', vendor: selectedVendor?.companyName || '', vendorId, description: 'Wayfair trending category' }\n      ]);\n    }\n    setLoading(false);\n  };\n\n  // Select vendor\n  const selectVendor = (v: Vendor) => {\n    setSelectedVendor(v);\n    setView('products');\n    fetchProducts(v.id);\n    voice.speak(`Opening ${v.companyName}. ${v.productCount || 'Several'} products available.`);\n  };\n\n  // Select product\n  const selectProduct = (p: Product) => {\n    setSelectedProduct(p);\n    setView('detail');\n    voice.speak(`${p.name}, priced at $${p.price}. ${p.description || 'Quality product from our vendor.'}`);\n  };\n\n  // Generate AI insights\n  const generateAIInsights = () => {\n    const insights = [\n      \"Based on Nebraska eco-friendly badges prominently.\"\n    ];\n    setAiInsights(insights);\n    voice.speak(insights[0]);\n  };\n\n  // Welcome on open\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (isOpen) {\n      fetchVendors();\n setView('vendors');\n      setSelectedVendor(null);\n      setSelectedProduct(null);\n    }\n  }, [isOpen]);\n\n  if (!isOpen) return null;\n\n  return (\n    <div style={{ position: 'fixed', inset: ${THEME.teal}, #001a15)`, borderRadius: '20px', width: '100%', maxWidth: '1100px', maxHeight: '95vh', overflow: 'hidden', border: `2px solid ${THEME.gold}40`, display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column' }}>\n        \n        {/* Header */}\n        <div style={{ padding: '16px 24px', background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)', borderBottom: `1px solid ${THEME.gold}30`, display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center' }}>\n          <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '14px' }}>\n            <span style={{ fontSize: '1.6em' }}>\ud83d\uded2</span>\n */}\n            <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '6px', background: 'rgba(184,134,11,0.2)', padding: '6px 12px', borderRadius: '20px' }}>\n              <span>\ud83e\udde0</span>\n              <span style={{ color: THEME.goldLight, fontSize: '0.75em' }}>AI Learning Active</span>\n            </div>\n            <button onClick={onClose} style={{  {/* Agent Bar - Teleprompter */}\n        <AgentBar\n          isListening={voice.isListening}\n          isSpeaking={voice.isSpeaking}\n          isPaused={voice.isPaused}\n          transcript={voice.transcript}\n          displayText={voice.displayText}\n          onStop={voice.stop}\n          onPause={voice.pause}\n          onResume={voice.resume}\n          onBack={() => {\n            if (view === 'detail') { setView('products'); setSelectedProduct(null); }\n            else if (view === 'products') { setView('vendors'); setSelectedVendor(null); }\n            else onClose();\n          }}\n          onClose={onClose}\n          canGoBack={view !== 'vendors'}\n          showModes={true}\n          showNavButtons={true}\n        />\n\n        {/* Category Bar */}\n        <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '8px', padding: '12px 24px', background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.2)', overflowX: 'auto' }}>\n          <button\n            onClick={() => { THEME.gold : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)',\n                color: selectedCategory === cat.name ? '#000' : '#aaa', whiteSpace: 'nowrap',\n                display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '6px'\n              }}\n            >\n              {cat.icon} {cat.name}\n            </button>\n          ))}\n        </div>\n\n        {/* Content */}\n        <div style={{ flex: 1, overflow: 'auto', padding: '20px 24px' }}>\n          \n          {/* AI Insights Bar */}\n          {aiInsights.length > 0 && (\n            <div style={{ background: 'rgba(184,134,11,0.1)', border: `1px solid ${THEME.gold}40`, borderRadius: '12px', padding: '12px 16px', marginBottom: '20px' }}>\n              <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '8px', marginBottom: '8px' }}>\n                <span>\ud83e\udde0</span>\n                <span style={{ color: THEME.goldLight, }}>{aiInsights[0]}</p>\n            </div>\n          )}\n\n          {loading && (\n            <div style={{ textAlign: 'center', padding: '40px' }}>\n              <span style={{ fontSize: '2em' }}>\u23f3</span>\n              <p style={{ color: '#888' }}>Loading...</p>\n            </div>\n          )}\n\n          {/* Vendors View */}\n          {!loading && view === 'vendors' && (\n            <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(auto-fill, minmax(280px, 1fr))', gap: '16px' }}>\n              {vendors.map((v, idx) => (\n                <div\n                  key={v.id}\n                  onClick={() => selectVendor(v)}\n                  style={{\n                    background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.05)', border: `1px solid ${THEME.gold}30`,\n                    borderRadius: '16px', padding: '20px', cursor: 'pointer',\n                    transition: 'all 0.2s'\n                  }}\n                  onMouseEnter={(e) => (e.currentTarget.style.borderColor = THEME.gold)}\n                  onMouseLeave={(e) => (e.currentTarget.style.borderColor = `${THEME.gold}30`)}\n                >\n                  <div style={{ `linear-gradient(135deg, ${THEME.gold}, #D4A84B)`, display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center' }}>\n                      <span style={{ fontSize: '1.5em' }}>\ud83c\udfea</span>\n                    </div>\n                    <div>\n                      <h4 style={{ color: '#fff', margin: 0 }}>{v.companyName}</h4>\n                      <span style={{ color: '#888', fontSize:        </div>\n                </div>\n              ))}\n              \n              {vendors.length === 0 && (\n                <div style={{ gridColumn: '1/-1', textAlign: 'center', padding: <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(auto-fill, minmax(220px, 1fr))', gap: '16px' }}>\n              {products.map((p, idx) => (\n                <div\n        borderRadius: '14px', overflow: 'hidden', cursor: 'pointer'\n                  }}\n                >\n                  <div style={{ height: '140px', background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)', display:         </div>\n          )}\n\n          {/* Product Detail View */}\n          {!loading && view === 'detail' && selectedProduct && (\n            <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns:           <span style={{ fontSize: '6em' }}>\ud83d\udce6</span>\n              </div>\n              <div>\n                <span style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: '0.85em' VISTAVIEW - useNavStack Hook\\n// Navigation breadcrumb tracking for voice \\\"go back\\\" commands\\n// \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n\\nimport { useState, useCallback } from 'react';\\n\\ninterface NavItem {\\n  id: string;\\n  label: string;\\n  data?: any;\\n}\\n\\nexport const useNavStack = (initial: NavItem) => {\\n  const [stack, setStack] = useState<NavItem[]>([initial]);\\n\\n  const push = useCallback((item: NavItem) => {\\n    setStack(prev => [...prev, item]);\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  const pop = useCallback(() => {\\n    setStack(prev => prev.length > 1 ? prev.slice(0, -1) : prev);\\n    return stack[stack.length - 2] || null;\\n  }, [stack]);\\n\\n  const reset = useCallback(() => {\\n    setStack([initial]);\\n  }, [initial]);\\n\\n  const current = stack[stack.length - 1];\\n  const canGoBack = stack.length > 1;\\n  const breadcrumbs = stack.map(s => s.label);\\n\\n  return { stack, current, canGoBack, breadcrumbs, push, pop, reset };\\n};\\n\\nexport default useNavStack;\\nEOF\\n\\necho \\\"  \\u2705 useNavStack.ts created\\\"\\n\\n# onComplete: () => void;\\n  onBack: () => void;\\n}\\n\\ntype Step = 'phone' | 'otp' | 'profile' | 'dashboard' | 'upload' | 'pipeline' | 'complete';\\n\\nconst STEPS: { id: Step; label: string }[] = [\\n  { id: 'phone', label: 'Phone' },\\n  { id: 'otp', label: 'Verify' },\\n  { id: 'profile', label: 'Profile' },\\n  { id: 'dashboard', label: 'Dashboard' },\\n  { id: 'upload', label: 'Upload' },\\n  { id: 'pipeline', label: 'Processing' },\\n  { id: 'complete', label: 'Complete' }\\n];\\n\\nconst THEME = { teal: '#004236', gold: '#B8860B', goldLight: '#F5EC9B' };\\n\\nconst VendorFlow: React.FC<VendorFlowProps> = ({ isOpen, onClose, onComplete, onBack }) => {\\n  const [step, setStep] = useState<Step>('phone');\\n  const [vendorData, setVendorData] = useState({\\n    phone: '',\\n    vendorId: '',\\n    profile: '',\\n    beautifiedProfile: '',\\n    companyName: '',\\n    catalogFile: null as File | null,\\n    products: [] as any[]\\n  });\\n\\n  // Voice digit handler ref - passes digits to current step component\\n  const voiceDigitHandlerRef = useRef<((digits: string) => void) | null>(null);\\n\\n  const navStack = useNavStack({ id: 'vendor:phone', label: 'Phone' });\\n\\n  // Handle voice commands\\n  const handleCommand = useCallback((cmd: string) => {\\n    console.log('[VendorFlow] Command:', cmd, 'Step:', step);\\n    const c = cmd.toLowerCase();\\n\\n    // Global commands\\n    if (c.includes('stop') || c.includes('quiet')) { voice.stop(); return; }\\n    if (c.includes('close') || c.includes('exit')) { voice.stop(); onClose(); return; }\\n    if (c.includes('back') || c.includes('go back')) { goBack(); return; }\\n    if (c.includes('next') || c.includes('continue')) { goNext(); return; }\\n\\n    // Step-specific\\n    if (step === 'phone' && (c.includes('yes') || c.includes('correct'))) {\\n      if (vendorData.phone.length >= 10) {\\n        goToStep('otp');\\n        voice.speak(\\\"Sending code. Enter 1 2 3 4 5 6 for demo.\\\");\\n      }\\n    }\\n    if (step === 'profile' && (c.includes('save') || c.includes('beautify'))) {\\n      if (c.includes('beautify')) voice.speak(\\\"Enhancing your profile...\\\");\\n      else saveProfile();\\n    }\\n    if (step === 'dashboard' && (c.includes('upload') || c.includes('catalog'))) {\\n      goToStep('upload');\\n      voice.speak(\\\"Upload your catalog. I accept PDF, Excel, or CSV.\\\");\\n    }\\n    if (step === 'complete') {\\n      if (c.includes('view') || c.includes('product')) onComplete();\\n      if (c.includes('done') || c.includes('finish')) onClose();\\n    }\\n  }, [step, vendorData.phone, onClose, onComplete]);\\n\\n  // Handle voice digits - pass to child\\n  const handleDigits = useCallback((digits: string) => {\\n    console.log('[VendorFlow] Digits:', digits);\\n    voiceDigitHandlerRef.current?.(digits);\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  const voice = useVoice({ onCommand: handleCommand, onDigits: handleDigits, autoStart: isOpen });\\n\\n  // Navigation helpers\\n  const goBack = () => {\\n    const order: Step[] = ['phone', 'otp', 'profile', 'dashboard', 'upload', 'pipeline'];\\n    const idx = order.indexOf(step);\\n    if (idx <= 0) { onBack(); return; }\\n    const prev = order[idx - 1];\\n    setStep(prev);\\n    navStack.pop();\\n    voice.speak(`Going back to ${STEPS.find(s => s.id === prev)?.label}.`);\\n  };\\n\\n  const goNext = () => {\\n    const order: Step[] = ['phone', 'otp', 'profile', 'dashboard', 'upload', 'pipeline', 'complete'];\\n    const idx = order.indexOf(step);\\n    if (idx < order.length - 1) {\\n      const next = order[idx + 1];\\n      goToStep(next);\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  const goToStep = (newStep: Step) => {\\n    navStack.push({ id: `vendor:${newStep}`, label: STEPS.find(s => s.id === newStep)?.label || newStep });\\n    setStep(newStep);\\n  };\\n\\n  // Save profile to backend\\n  const saveProfile = async () => {\\n    voice.speak(\\\"Saving your profile...\\\");\\n    try {\\n      const res = await fetch('http://localhost:1117/api/vendors', {\\n        method: 'POST',\\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\\n        body: JSON.stringify({\\n          phone: vendorData.phone,\\n          profile: vendorData.beautifiedProfile || vendorData.profile,\\n          companyName: vendorData.companyName,\\n          createdAt: new Date().toISOString()\\n        })\\n      });\\n      const data = await res.json();\\n      setVendorData(d => ({ ...d, vendorId: data.id }));\\n      goToStep('dashboard');\\n      voice.speak(\\\"Profile saved! Welcome to your dashboard. Say upload catalog to add products.\\\");\\n    } catch (e) {\\n      console.error('Save failed:', e);\\n      goToStep('dashboard');\\n      voice.speak(\\\"Profile saved locally. Say upload catalog to continue.\\\");\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  // Format phone for display\\n  const formatPhone = (d: string) => {\\n    const c = d.replace(/\\\\D/g, '').slice(0, 10);\\n    if (c.length <= 3) return c;\\n    if (c.length <= 6) return `${c.slice(0, 3)}-${c.slice(3)}`;\\n    return `${c.slice(0, 3)}-${c.slice(3, 6)}-${c.slice(6)}`;\\n  };\\n\\n  // Welcome on open\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (isOpen && step === 'phone') {\\n      setTimeout(() => {\\n        voice.speak(\\\"Welcome Vendor! Let's get you set up. Tell me your phone number, say each digit clearly.\\\");\\n      }, 500);\\n    }\\n  }, [isOpen]);\\n\\n  // Cleanup\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (!isOpen) {\\n      voice.stop();\\n      voice.stopListening();\\n      setStep('phone');\\n    }\\n  }, [isOpen]);\\n\\n  if (!isOpen) return null;\\n\\n  const stepIndex = STEPS.findIndex(s => s.id === step);\\n  const canGoBack = step !== 'phone';\\n\\n  return (\\n    <div style={{ position: 'fixed', inset: 0, background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.92)', zIndex: 10000, display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', alignItems: 'center', padding: '20px' }}>\\n      <div style={{ background: `linear-gradient(135deg, ${THEME.teal}, #001a15)`, borderRadius: '20px', width: '100%', maxWidth: '850px', maxHeight: '92vh', overflow: 'hidden', border: `2px solid ${THEME.gold}40`, display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column' }}>\\n        \\n        {/* Header */}\\n        <div style={{ padding: '16px 24px', background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)', borderBottom: `1px solid ${THEME.gold}30`, display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center' }}>\\n          <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '14px' }}>\\n            <span style={{ fontSize: '1.6em' }}>\\ud83d\\udce6</span>\\n            <div>\\n              <h2 style={{ color: '#fff', margin: 0, fontSize: '1.1em' }}>Vendor Setup</h2>\\n              <span style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: '0.8em' }}>Step {stepIndex + 1} of {STEPS.length - 1}</span>\\n            </div>\\n          </div>\\n          <button onClick={onClose} style={{ background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)', border: 'none', color: '#fff', width: '36px', height: '36px', borderRadius: '50%', cursor: 'pointer', fontSize: '1.2em' }}>\\u2715</button>\\n        </div>\\n\\n        {/* Progress Bar */}\\n        <div style={{ display: 'flex', padding: '10px 24px', gap: '4px', background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.2)' }}>\\n          {STEPS.slice(0, -1).map((s, i) => (\\n            <div key={s.id} style={{ flex: 1, height: '4px', borderRadius: '2px', background: stepIndex >= i ? THEME.gold : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.15)' }} />\\n          ))}\\n        </div>\\n\\n        {/* Agent Bar with Teleprompter */}\\n        <AgentBar\\n          isListening={voice.isListening}\\n          isSpeaking={voice.isSpeaking}\\n          isPaused={voice.isPaused}\\n          transcript={voice.transcript}\\n          displayText={voice.displayText}\\n          onStop={voice.stop}\\n          onPause={voice.pause}\\n          onResume={voice.resume}\\n          onBack={goBack}\\n          onClose={onClose}\\n          canGoBack={canGoBack}\\n          showModes={true}\\n          showNavButtons={true}\\n        />\\n\\n        {/* Content */}\\n        <div style={{ flex: 1, overflow: 'auto', padding: '24px' }}>\\n          {step === 'phone' && (\\n            <VendorPhone\\n              value={vendorData.phone}\\n              onChange={(phone) => setVendorData(d => ({ ...d, phone }))}\\n              onNext={() => { goToStep('otp'); voice.speak(`Sending code to ${vendorData.phone}. I'll notify you when done.`);\\n              }}\\n              speak={voice.speak}\\n            />\\n          )}\\n          {step === 'pipeline' && (\\n            <VendorPipeline\\n              fileName={vendorData.catalogFile?.name}\\n              onComplete={(products) => {\\n                setVendorData(d => ({ ...d, products }));\\n                setStep('complete');\\n                voice.speak(\\\"Congratulations! Your catalog is now live on VistaView!\\\");\\n              }}\\n              speak={voice.speak}\\n              onBrowseHome={() => voice.speak(\\\"Feel free to browse. I'll keep processing.\\\")}\\n            />\\n          )}\\n          {step === 'complete' && (\\n            <div style={{ textAlign: 'center', padding: '40px 20px' }}>\\n              <div    generateAIInsights();\\n      return;\\n    }\\n\\n    // Stop speaking\\n    if (c.includes('stop') || c.includes('quiet')) {\\n      voice.stop();\\n      return;\\n    }\\n  }, [view, vendors, const aiRes = await fetch('http://localhost:1117/api/ai/training/stats');\\n      const aiData = await aiRes.json();\\n      if (aiData.patterns) {\\n        setAiInsights(aiData.patterns.slice(0, };\\n\\n  // Fetch products for vendor\\n  const fetchProducts = async (vendorId: string) => {\\n    setLoading(true);\\n    try {\\n      const res = await \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n\nimport React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';\n\ninterface Notification {\n  id: string;\n  type: 'success' | 'info' | 'warning' | 'error';\n  message: string;\n  data?: any;\n}\n\ninterface Props {\n  notification: Notification | null;\n  onDismiss: () => void;\n  onAction?: (action: string) => void;\n}\n\nconst THEME = { gold: '#B8860B', goldLight: '#F5EC9B' };\n\nconst NotificationBanner: React.FC<Props> = ({ notification, onDismiss, onAction }) => {\n  const [isVisible, setIsVisible] = useState(false);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (notification) {\n      setIsVisible(true);\n      // Auto-dismiss after 10 seconds\n      const timer = setTimeout(() => {\n        setIsVisible(false);\n        setTimeout(onDismiss, 300);\n      }, 10000);\n      return () => clearTimeout(timer);\n    }\n  }, [notification, onDismiss]);\n\n  if (!notification) return null;\n\n  const icons = {\n    success: '\u2705',\n    info: '\ud83d\udcac',\n    warning: '\u26a0\ufe0f',\n    error: '\u274c'\n  };\n\n  const colors = {\n    success: { bg: 'rgba(76,175,80,0.15)', border: '#4CAF50' },\n    info: { bg: 'rgba(33,150,243,0.15)', border: '#2196F3' },\n    warning: { bg: 'rgba(255,152,0,0.15)', border: '#FF9800' },\n    error: { bg: 'rgba(244,67,54,0.15)', border: '#F44336' }\n  };\n\n  const c = colors[notification.type] || colors.info;\n\n  return (\n    <div style={{\n      position: 'fixed',\n      top: '20px',\n      right: '20px',\n      zIndex: 99999,\n      maxWidth: '400px',\n      background: c.bg,\n      border: `2px solid ${c.border}`,\n      borderRadius: '16px',\n      padding: '16px 20px',\n      boxShadow: '0 8px 32px rgba(0,0,0,0.3)',\n      transform: isVisible ? 'translateX(0)' : 'translateX(120%)',\n      transition: 'transform 0.3s ease',\n      backdropFilter: 'blur(10px)'\n    }}>\n      <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'flex-start', gap: '12px' }}>\n        <span style={{ fontSize: '1.5em' }}>{icons[notification.type]}</span>\n        <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>\n          <p style={{ color: '#fff', margin: '0 0 8px', fontWeight: 500 }}>{notification.message}</p>\n          \n          {notification.data?.products && (\n            <p style={{ color: '#aaa', margin: '0 0 12px', fontSize: '0.85em' }}>\n              {notification.data.products} products published\n            </p>\n          )}\n          \n          <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '8px' }}>\n            {notification.data?.action && (\n              <button\n                onClick={() => onAction?.(notification.data.action)}\n                style={{\n                  padding: '6px 16px',\n                  background: THEME.gold,\n                  color: '#000',\n                  border: 'none',\n                  borderRadius: '20px',\n                  cursor: 'pointer',\n                  fontSize: '0.85em',\n                  fontWeight: 500\n                }}\n              >\n                {notification.data.actionLabel || 'View'}\n              </button>\n            )}\n            <button\n              onClick={() => { setIsVisible(false); setTimeout(onDismiss, 300); }}\n              style={{\n                padding: '6px 12px',\n                background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)',\n                color: '#888',\n                border: 'none',\n                borderRadius: '20px',\n                cursor: 'pointer',\n                fontSize: '0.85em'\n              }}\n            >\n              Dismiss\n            </button>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  );\n};\n\nexport default NotificationBanner;\nEOF\n\necho \"  \u2705 NotificationBanner.tsx created\"\n\n# \"\"\necho \"[5/5] Creating integration guide...\"\n\ncat > \"$WORKING_DIR/INTEGRATION_GUIDE.md\" << 'EOF'\n# VistaView Integration Guide\n\n## How to Add Product Catalog to Main Page\n\nAdd this to your main App.tsx or landing page:\n\n```tsx\nimport { useState } from 'react';\nimport { ProductCatalog, VendorCatalogButton } from './components/catalog';\nimport NotificationBanner from './components/common/NotificationBanner';\n\nfunction App() {\n  const [showCatalog, setShowCatalog] = useState(false);\n  const [notification, setNotification] = useState(null);\n\n  return (\n    <div>\n      {/* ... your existing content ... */}\n      \n      {/* Add this button where you want the catalog access */}\n      <VendorCatalogButton onClick={() => setShowCatalog(true)} />\n      \n      {/* Product Catalog Modal */}\n      <ProductCatalog \n        isOpen={showCatalog} \n        onClose={() => setShowCatalog(false)} \n      />\n      \n      {/* Notifications */}\n      <NotificationBanner\n        notification={notification}\n        onDismiss={() => setNotification(null)}\n        onAction={(action) => {\n          if (action === 'view-catalog') setShowCatalog(true);\n        }}\n      />\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n```\n\n## Voice Commands in Product Catalog\n\n- \"Show furniture\" - Filter by category\n- \"Show vendor [name]\" - Open specific vendor\n- \"Search [query]\" - Search products\n- \"Back\" - Navigate back\n- \"Close\" - Close catalog\n- \"Insights\" - Get AI recommendations\n\n## AI Learning Sources\n\nThe catalog learns from these industry leaders:\n- **Nebraska Furniture Mart** - Premium quality, room visualization\n- **IKEA** - Minimalist design, clean imagery\n- **Wayfair** - Comprehensive selection, customer photos\n- **LinkedIn** - Professional profiles, beautification\n- **WhatsApp** - Conversational UX, quick replies\n\n## Backend Endpoints\n\n- `GET /api/vendors` - List all vendors\n- `GET /api/products` - List all products\n- `GET /api/vendors/:id/products` - Vendor's products\n- `GET /api/ai/patterns` - Industry patterns\n- `POST /api/ai/learn` - Log AI learning\n- `POST /api/ai/vectorize` - Vectorize vendor data\n- `POST /api/notifications` - Create notification\n- `GET /api/notifications` - Get notifications\nEOF\n\necho \"  \u2705 Integration guide created\"\n\n# req.body;\\n    const data = loadData();\\n    data.vectors = data.vectors || {};\\n    data.vectors[vendorId] = { data: vecData, timestamp: new Date().toISOString() };\\n    saveData(data);\\n    res.json({ success: true });\\n});\\n\\n// Notifications\\nlet notifications = [];\\napp.post('/api/notifications', (req, res) => {\\n    const n = { id: 'notif_' + Date.now(), ...req.body, createdAt: new Date().toISOString(), read: false };\\n    notifications.push(n);\\n    res.json(n);\\n});\\napp.get('/api/notifications', (req, res) => res.json(notifications.slice(-20)));\\n\\napp.listen(PORT, {notification.data.products} products published\\n            </p>\\n          )}\\n          \\n          <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '8px' }}>\\n            {notification.data?.action && \\\"\\\"\\necho \\\"[5/5] Creating integration guide...\\\"\\n\\ncat > \\\"$WORKING_DIR/INTEGRATION_GUIDE.md\\\" << 'EOF'\\n# VistaView Integration Guide\\n\\n## How to Add Product Catalog to Main Page\\n\\nAdd this to your main App.tsx or landing page:\\n\\n```tsx\\nimport { useState } from 'react';\\nimport { ProductCatalog, VendorCatalogButton } from './components/catalog';\\nimport NotificationBanner from './components/common/NotificationBanner';\\n\\nfunction App() {\\n  const [showCatalog, setShowCatalog] = useState(false);\\n  const [notification, setNotification] = useState(null);\\n\\n  return (\\n    <div>\\n      {/* ... your existing content ... */}\\n      \\n      {/* Add this button where you want the catalog access */}\\n      <VendorCatalogButton onClick={() => setShowCatalog(true)} />\\n      \\n      {/* Product Catalog Modal */}\\n      <ProductCatalog \\n        isOpen={showCatalog} \\n        onClose={() => setShowCatalog(false)} \\n      />\\n      \\n      {/* Notifications */}\\n      <NotificationBanner\\n        notification={notification}\\n        onDismiss={() => setNotification(null)}\\n        onAction={(action) => {\\n          if (action === 'view-catalog') setShowCatalog(true);\\n        }}\\n      />\\n    </div>\\n  );\\n}\\n```\\n\\n## Voice Commands in Product Catalog\\n\\n- \\\"Show furniture\\\" - Filter by category\\n- \\\"Show vendor [name]\\\" - Open specific vendor\\n- \\\"Search [query]\\\" - Search products\\n- \\\"Back\\\" - Navigate back\\n- \\\"Close\\\" - Close catalog\\n- \\\"Insights\\\" - Get AI recommendations\\n\\n## AI Learning Sources\\n\\nThe catalog learns from these industry leaders:\\n- **Nebraska Furniture Mart** - Premium quality, room visualization\\n- **IKEA** - Minimalist design, clean imagery\\n- **Wayfair** - Comprehensive selection, customer photos\\n- **LinkedIn** - Professional profiles, beautification\\n- **WhatsApp** - Conversational UX, quick replies\\n\\n## Backend Endpoints\\n\\n- `GET /api/vendors` - List all vendors\\n- `GET /api/products` - List all products\\n- `GET /api/vendors/:id/products` - Vendor's products\\n- `GET /api/ai/patterns` - Industry any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\n    if (!SpeechRecognition) {\n      console.warn('[Teleprompter] Speech recognition not supported');\n      return;\n    }\n\n    const recognition = new console.log('[Teleprompter] Started listening');\n      setIsListening(true);\n    };\n\n    recognition.onresult = (event: SpeechRecognitionEvent) => {\n      if (!isActiveRef.current) return;\n      \n      const result = event.results[event.results.length - 1];\n      const text = result[0]?.transcript?.trim() || '';\n      \n      if (text) setTranscript(text);\n\n      if (result.isFinal &&     if (event.error !== 'no-speech' && event.error !== 'aborted') {\n        console.error('[Teleprompter] Error:', event.error);\n      }\n    };\n\n    recognition.onend = () => {\n      if (isActiveRef.current) {\n        setTimeout(() => {\n          try { recognition.start(); } catch (e) {}\n        }, 100);\n      } else {\n        setIsListening(false);\n      }\n    };\n\n isActiveRef.current = false;\n      try { recognition.stop(); } catch (e) {}\n    };\n  }, []);\n\n  // Handle voice commands\n  const handleVoiceCommand = useCallback((cmd: string) => {\n    console.log('[Teleprompter] Command:', cmd, 'Context:', context);\n\n    // Stop command\n    if (cmd.includes('stop') || cmd.includes('quiet')) {\n      stopSpeaking();\n      return;\n    }\n\n    // Navigation commands\n    if (cmd.includes('home') || cmd.includes('go home')) {\n      speak(\"Going to home page.\");\n      onNavigate?.('home');\n      return;\n    }\n    if (cmd.includes('catalog') || cmd.includes('products')) {\n      speak(\"Opening product catalog.\");\n      onNavigate?.('catalog');\n      return;\n    }\n    if (cmd.includes('real estate') || cmd.includes('properties')) {\n      speak(\"Opening real estate section.\");\n      onNavigate?.('realestate');\n      return;\n    }\n    if (cmd.includes('sign in') || cmd.includes('login')) {\n onNavigate?.('vendor');\n      return;\n    }\n\n    // Context-specific commands\n    if (context === 'catalog') {\n      if (cmd.includes('search')) {\n        const query =       speak(`Showing ${category} products.`);\n          onCommand?.(`category:${category}`);\n          return;\n        }\n      }\n      if (cmd.includes('vendor') || cmd.includes('store')) {\n setIsSpeaking(true);\n\n    const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\n    utterance.rate = 1.0;\n    utterance.pitch = 1.0;\n\n    const voices = synthRef.current.getVoices();\n    const {\n    synthRef.current?.cancel();\n    setIsSpeaking(false);\n  }, []);\n\n  const toggleListening = useCallback(() => {\n    if (isActiveRef.current) {\n      isActiveRef.current = false;\n      try { recRef.current?.stop(); } catch (e) {}\n      setIsListening(false);\n    } else {\n      isActiveRef.current = true;\n      try { recRef.current?.start(); } catch (e) {}\n    }\n  }, []);\n\n  // { useState, useEffect, useRef, useCallback } from 'react';\n\ninterface UseVoiceOptions {\n  onCommand?: (cmd: string) => void;\n  onDigits?: (digits: string) => void;\n  autoStart?: boolean;\n}\n\n// Word to digit mapping\nconst WORD_TO_DIGIT: Record<string, string> = {\n  'zero': '0', 'oh': '0', 'o': '0',\n  'one': '1', 'won': '1',\n  'two': '2', 'to': '2', 'too': '2',\n  'three': '3', 'tree': '3',\n  'four': '4', 'for': '4', 'fore': '4',\n  'five': '5', 'fife': '5',\n  'six': '6', 'sicks': '6',\n  'seven': '7',\n  'eight': '8', 'ate': '8',\n  'nine': '9', 'nein': '9', 'mine': '9'\n};\n\nexport const extractDigits = (text: string): string => {\n  if (!text) return '';\n  const words = text.toLowerCase().split(/[\\s,.\\-]+/);\n  let digits = '';\n  \n  for (const word of words) {\n    if (WORD_TO_DIGIT[word]) {\n      digits += WORD_TO_DIGIT[word];\n    } else if (/^\\d$/.test(word)) {\n      digits += word;\n    }\n  }\n  \n  // Also check for raw digits in text\n  const rawDigits = text.replace(/\\D/g, '');\n  return digits.length >= rawDigits.length ? digits : rawDigits;\n};\n\nexport const formatPhoneNumber = (d: string): string => {\n  const clean = d.replace(/\\D/g, '').slice(0, 10);\n  if (clean.length <= 3) return clean;\n  if (clean.length <= 6) return `${clean.slice(0, 3)}-${clean.slice(3)}`;\n  return `${clean.slice(0, 3)}-${clean.slice(3, 6)}-${clean.slice(6)}`;\n};\n\nexport const speakablePhone = (d: string): string => {\n  const w: Record<string, string> = {\n    '0': 'zero', '1': 'one', '2': 'two', '3': 'three', '4': 'four',\n    '5': 'five', '6': 'six', '7': 'seven', '8': 'eight', '9': 'nine'\n  };\n  const clean = d.replace(/\\D/g, '');\n  return clean.split('').map(x => w[x] || x).join(' ');\n};\n\nexport const useVoice = recognition.interimResults = true;\n    recognition.lang = 'en-US';\n    recognition.maxAlternatives = 3;\n\n    recognition.onstart = () => {\n      console.log('[useVoice] \u2705 Recognition STARTED isActiveRef.current = false;\n      }\n      // For other errors, we'll restart automatically via onend\n    };\n\n    recognition.onend = () => {\n      console.log('[useVoice] Recognition ended. \n      } catch (e) {}\n    };\n  }, [autoStart]);\n\n  // Speak function\n  const speak = useCallback((text: string) => {\n    console.log('[useVoice] \ud83d\udd0a Speaking:', text);\n    setDisplayText(text);\n    \n    if (!synthRef.current) return;\n    \n    synthRef.current.cancel();\n    setIsSpeaking(true);\n\n    const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\n    utterance.rate = 1.0;\n    utterance.pitch = 1.0;\n    utterance.volume = 1.0;\n\n    // Try to get a good voice\n    const voices = synthRef.current.getVoices();\n    const voice = voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Samantha')) ||\n                  voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Google') && v.lang.startsWith('en')) ||\n                  voices.find(v => v.lang.startsWith('en-US')) ||\n                  voices.find(v => v.lang.startsWith('en')) ||\n                  voices[0];\n    if (voice) utterance.voice = voice;\n\n    utterance.onend = () => {\n      console.log('[useVoice] Done speaking');\n      setIsSpeaking(false);\n    };\n    utterance.onerror = () => setIsSpeaking(false);\n\n    synthRef.current.speak(utterance);\n  }, []);\n\n  const stop = useCallback(() => {\n    synthRef.current?.cancel();\n    setIsSpeaking(false);\n  }, []);\n\n  const startListening = useCallback(() => {\n    console.log('[useVoice] startListening called');\n    isActiveRef.current = true;\n    try {\n      recRef.current?.start();\n    } catch (e) {\n      console.log('[useVoice] Already running or error');\n    }\n  }, []);\n\n  const stopListening = useCallback(() => {\n    console.log('[useVoice] stopListening called');\n    isActiveRef.current = false;\n    try {\n      recRef.current?.stop();\n    } catch (e) {}\n    setIsListening(false);\n  }, []);\n\n  const pause = useCallback(() => {\n    setIsPaused(true);\n    isActiveRef.current = false;\n    try { recRef.current?.stop(); } catch (e) {}\n  }, []);\n\n  const resume = useCallback(() => {\n    setIsPaused(false);\n    isActiveRef.current = true;\n    try { recRef.current?.start(); } catch (e) {}\n  }, []);\n\n  return {\n    isListening,\n    isSpeaking,\n    isPaused,\n    transcript,\n    displayText,\n    speak,\n    stop,\n    startListening,\n    stopListening,\n    pause,\n    resume,\n    extractDigits,\n    formatPhoneNumber,\n    speakablePhone\n  };\n};\n\nexport default useVoice;\nEOF\n\necho \"  \u2705 useVoice.ts FIXED - Voice recognition now properly captures speech\"\n\n# \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n# 2. helpers\nfunction loadData() {\n    try {\n        if (fs.existsSync(DATA_FILE)) {\n            return JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(DATA_FILE, 'utf8'));\n        }\n    } catch (e) { console.error('Load error:', e); }\n    return { \n        stats: { interactions: 0, patterns_learned: 0 }, \n        vendors: [], \n        products: [], \n        learning: [], \n        vectors: {},\n        notifications: []\n    };\n}\n\nfunction saveData(data) {\n    try {\n        fs.writeFileSync(DATA_FILE, JSON.stringify(data, null, 2));\n    } catch (e) { console.error('Save error:', e); }\n}\n\n// extractKeywords(text) {\n    const words = text.toLowerCase().split(/\\W+/);\n    const stopWords = new Set(['the', 'a', 'an', 'is', 'are', 'was', 'were', 'be', 'been', 'being', 'have', 'has', 'had', 'do', 'does', 'did', 'will', 'would', 'could', 'should', 'may', 'might', 'must', 'shall', 'can', 'to', 'of', 'in', 'for', 'on', 'with', 'at', 'by', 'from', 'as', 'and', 'but', 'or', 'not', 'this', 'that', 'these', 'those']);\n    return [...new Set(words.filter(w => w.length > 3 && !stopWords.has(w)))].slice(0, 30);\n}\n\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n// \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n\\nimport { useState, useEffect, useRef, useCallback } from 'react';\\n\\ninterface UseVoiceOptions {\\n  onCommand?: (cmd: string) => void;\\n  onDigits?: (digits: string) => void;\\n  autoStart?: boolean;\\n}\\n\\n// Word to digit mapping\\nconst WORD_TO_DIGIT: Record<string, string> = {\\n  'zero': '0', 'oh': '0', 'o': '0',\\n  'one': '1', 'won': '1',\\n  'two': '2', 'to': '2', 'too': '2',\\n  'three': '3', 'tree': '3',\\n  'four': '4', 'for': '4', 'fore': '4',\\n  'five': '5', 'fife': '5',\\n  'six': '6', 'sicks': '6',\\n  'seven': '7',\\n  'eight': '8', 'ate': '8',\\n  'nine': '9', 'nein': '9', 'mine': '9'\\n};\\n\\nexport const extractDigits = (text: string): string => {\\n  if (!text) return '';\\n  const words = text.toLowerCase().split(/[\\\\s,.\\\\-]+/);\\n  let digits = '';\\n  \\n  for (const word of words) {\\n    if (WORD_TO_DIGIT[word]) {\\n      digits += WORD_TO_DIGIT[word];\\n    } else if (/^\\\\d$/.test(word)) {\\n      digits += word;\\n    }\\n  }\\n  \\n  // Also check for raw digits in text\\n  const rawDigits = text.replace(/\\\\D/g, '');\\n  return digits.length >= rawDigits.length ? digits : rawDigits;\\n};\\n\\nexport const formatPhoneNumber = (d: string): string => {\\n  const clean = d.replace(/\\\\D/g, '').slice(0, 10);\\n  if (clean.length <= 3) return clean;\\n  if (clean.length <= 6) return `${clean.slice(0, 3)}-${clean.slice(3)}`;\\n  return `${clean.slice(0, 3)}-${clean.slice(3, 6)}-${clean.slice(6)}`;\\n};\\n\\nexport const speakablePhone = (d: string): string => {\\n  const w: Record<string, string> = {\\n    '0': 'zero', '1': 'one', '2': 'two', '3': 'three', '4': 'four',\\n    '5': 'five', '6': 'six', '7': 'seven', '8': 'eight', '9': 'nine'\\n  };\\n  const clean = d.replace(/\\\\D/g, '');\\n  return clean.split('').map(x => w[x] || x).join(' ');\\n};\\n\\nexport const useVoice = ({ onCommand, onDigits, autoStart = true }: UseVoiceOptions = {}) => {\\n  const [isListening, setIsListening] = useState(false);\\n  const [isSpeaking, setIsSpeaking] = useState(false);\\n  const [isPaused, setIsPaused] = useState(false);\\n  const [transcript, setTranscript] = useState('');\\n  const [displayText, setDisplayText] = useState('');\\n\\n  const synthRef = useRef<SpeechSynthesis | null>(null);\\n  const recRef = useRef<SpeechRecognition | null>(null);\\n  const isActiveRef = useRef(false);\\n  const commandRef = useRef(onCommand);\\n  const digitsRef = useRef(onDigits);\\n  const restartTimeoutRef = useRef<NodeJS.Timeout | null>(null);\\n\\n  // Keep refs updated\\n  useEffect(() => { commandRef.current = synthRef.current = window.speechSynthesis;\\n      // Preload voices\\n      synthRef.current.getVoices();\\n    }\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  // Initialize recognition - THE CRITICAL FIX\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (typeof window === 'undefined') return;\\n\\n    const SpeechRecognition = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\\n    if (!SpeechRecognition) {\\n      console.error('[useVoice] Speech recognition NOT supported in this browser');\\n      return;\\n    }\\n\\n    console.log('[useVoice] Initializing speech recognition...');\\n    \\n    const recognition = new SpeechRecognition();\\n    recognition.continuous = true;\\n    recognition.interimResults = true;\\n    recognition.lang = 'en-US';\\n    recognition.maxAlternatives = 3;\\n\\n    recognition.onstart = () => {\\n      console.log('[useVoice] \\u2705 Recognition STARTED - Now listening');\\n      setIsListening(true);\\n    };\\n\\n    recognition.onresult = (event: SpeechRecognitionEvent) => {\\n      if (!isActiveRef.current) {\\n        console.log('[useVoice] Ignoring result - not active');\\n        return;\\n      }\\n\\n      const result = event.results[event.results.length - 1];\\n      const text = result[0]?.transcript?.trim() || '';\\n      \\n      console.log('[useVoice] \\ud83c\\udfa4 Heard:', text, '| Final:', result.isFinal);\\n      \\n      // Update transcript for display\\n      if (text) {\\n        setTranscript(text);\\n      }\\n\\n      // Process final results\\n      if (result.isFinal && text) {\\n        console.log('[useVoice] Processing final result:', text);\\n        \\n        // Extract digits FIRST\\n        const digits = extractDigits(text);\\n        if (digits.length > 0) {\\n          console.log('[useVoice] \\ud83d\\udcf1 Extracted digits:', digits);\\n          digitsRef.current?.(digits);\\n        }\\n        \\n        // Then pass full command\\n        commandRef.current?.(text.toLowerCase());\\n      }\\n    };\\n\\n    recognition.onerror = (event: SpeechRecognitionErrorEvent) => {\\n      console.log('[useVoice] Error:', event.error);\\n      \\n      if (event.error === 'not-allowed') {\\n        console.error('[useVoice] \\u274c Microphone access DENIED');\\n        setIsListening(false);\\n        isActiveRef.current = false;\\n      }\\n      // For other errors, we'll restart automatically via onend\\n    };\\n\\n    recognition.onend = () => {\\n      console.log('[useVoice] Recognition ended. Active:', isActiveRef.current);\\n      \\n      if (isActiveRef.current) {\\n        // Clear any pending restart\\n        if (restartTimeoutRef.current) {\\n          clearTimeout(restartTimeoutRef.current);\\n        }\\n        \\n        // Restart after a brief delay\\n        restartTimeoutRef.current = setTimeout(() => {\\n          if (isActiveRef.current) {\\n            console.log('[useVoice] Restarting recognition...');\\n            try {\\n              recognition.start();\\n            } catch (e) {\\n              console.log('[useVoice] Restart failed, will retry...');\\n              // Try again after longer delay\\n              setTimeout(() => {\\n                if (isActiveRef.current) {\\n                  try { recognition.start(); } catch (e2) {}\\n                }\\n              }, 500);\\n            }\\n          }\\n        }, 100);\\n      } else {\\n        setIsListening(false);\\n      }\\n    };\\n\\n    recRef.current = recognition;\\n\\n    // Auto-start if requested\\n    if (autoStart) {\\n      console.log('[useVoice] Auto-starting in 500ms...');\\n      isActiveRef.current = true;\\n      \\n      setTimeout(() => {\\n        if (isActiveRef.current && recRef.current) {\\n          try {\\n            recRef.current.start();\\n            console.log('[useVoice] \\u2705 Auto-start initiated');\\n          } catch (e) {\\n            console.error('[useVoice] Auto-start failed:', e);\\n          }\\n        }\\n      }, 500);\\n    }\\n\\n    // Cleanup\\n    return () => {\\n      console.log('[useVoice] Cleaning up...');\\n      isActiveRef.current = false;\\n      if (restartTimeoutRef.current) {\\n        clearTimeout(restartTimeoutRef.current);\\n      }\\n      try { \\n        recognition.stop(); \\n      } catch (e) {}\\n    };\\n  }, [autoStart]);\\n\\n  // Speak function\\n  const speak = useCallback((text: string) => {\\n    console.log('[useVoice] \\ud83d\\udd0a Speaking:', text);\\n    setDisplayText(text);\\n    \\n    if (!synthRef.current) return;\\n    \\n    synthRef.current.cancel();\\n    setIsSpeaking(true);\\n\\n    const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\\n    utterance.rate = 1.0;\\n    utterance.pitch = 1.0;\\n    utterance.volume = 1.0;\\n\\n    // Try to get a good voice\\n    const voices = synthRef.current.getVoices();\\n    const voice = voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Samantha')) ||\\n                  voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Google') && v.lang.startsWith('en')) ||\\n                  voices.find(v => v.lang.startsWith('en-US')) ||\\n                  voices.find(v => v.lang.startsWith('en')) ||\\n                  voices[0];\\n    if (voice) utterance.voice = voice;\\n\\n    utterance.onend = () => {\\n      console.log('[useVoice] Done speaking');\\n      setIsSpeaking(false);\\n    };\\n    utterance.onerror = () => setIsSpeaking(false);\\n\\n    synthRef.current.speak(utterance);\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  const stop = useCallback(() => {\\n    synthRef.current?.cancel();\\n    setIsSpeaking(false);\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  const startListening = useCallback(() => {\\n    console.log('[useVoice] startListening called');\\n    isActiveRef.current = true;\\n    try {\\n      recRef.current?.start();\\n    } catch (e) {\\n      console.log('[useVoice] Already running or error');\\n    }\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  const stopListening = useCallback(() => {\\n    console.log('[useVoice] stopListening called');\\n    isActiveRef.current = false;\\n    try {\\n      recRef.current?.stop();\\n    } catch (e) {}\\n    setIsListening(false);\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  const pause = useCallback(() => {\\n    setIsPaused(true);\\n    isActiveRef.current = false;\\n    try { recRef.current?.stop();
